| <span data-ttu-id="112ef-1423">進入</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="112ef-1423">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="112ef-1424">值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="112ef-1424">Value</span></span> |
